Author of Al-Khulasa and His Works
Biographical notes on the author of Al-Khulasa

Learning Objective
By the end of this lesson, you will be able to state the scholarly rank of the author of Al-Khulasa and list his major works as mentioned in the passage.

Core Idea
Al-Khulasa's author was a mujtahid fi al-masa'il from Transoxiana, a peerless Hanafi chief.

Knowing the author's authority helps you evaluate the weight of his works in fatwa. This passage identifies him as a major figure from Transoxiana, classified as a mujtahid fi al-masa'il by Ibn Kamal Pasha.

Guided Path
1
Identify the author and his works
Read the passage to find the name of the author (though not given explicitly) and list his other books mentioned: Khazanat al-Fatawa, Khazanat al-Waqi'at, Nisab al-Faqih. Also note that Al-Khulasa is an abridgment of Al-Waqi'at and Al-Khazana.
2
Determine the author's scholarly rank
The passage classifies him as a mujtahid fi al-masa'il. Understand that this means he can perform ijtihad on new issues but cannot contradict the school's founder in usul and furu'.
This is the third level of Hanafi mujtahids, below mujtahid fi al-madhhab.
3
Locate his death year and geographical context
Find the death year (542 AH) and region (Transoxiana). This contextualizes him in the 6th century AH as a leading Hanafi scholar.
4
Assess the value of his works for fatwa
Recognize that his works are considered acceptable ("masmula") and that Al-Khulasa is a standard reference. A mufti should rely on his writings within the limits of his ijtihad rank.

Source Text
⚠ Extracted via Advanced OCR ∼97% accuracy, minor errors may remain — always verify against original Arabic books
تكتب الوان في السرح مع بيان مواضع المسائل وكتب فهرست الفصول والأحساس على رأس كل كتاب : ليكون عونا لمن ابتلى بالفتوى .. كذا في الكشف. وفيه تصريح يكون الخلاصة في مجلد مع أنه قد طبع في الهند في اربع مجلدات. وفى الكشف أيضا عند ذكر نصاب الفتيه أنه اختصر منه كتابه المسمى بخلاصة العناوي" . وقال مولانا عبد الحي في الفوائد أنه لخصه من الواقعات والخزانة ، فتدبر . واعلم أنه رحمه الله كان عديم النظير في ،زمانه فريد أئمة الدهر، شيخ الحنفية بما وراء النهر، ذكره المولى ابن كمال باشا الرومي من طبقة المجتهدين في المسائل الذين يقدرون على الاجتهاد في المسائل لا رواية فيها من صاحب المذهب، ولا يقدرون على مخالفته في الفروع والأصول. وله سوى الخلاصة تصانیف مقبولة منها : خزانة الفتاوى" و "خزانة الواقعات" ، و "نصاب الفقيه " . وأرخ صاحب الكشف وفاته عند ذكر تلك التصانيف سنة ٥٤٢هـ .
Various colors are written in the commentary with clarification of the places of the issues, and indexes of chapters and [؟] are written at the head of each book: to be a help for one who is tried with giving fatwa. Thus in Al-Kashf. And in it is an explicit statement that Al-Khulasa is in one volume, although it has been printed in India in four volumes. And in Al-Kashf also, when mentioning Nisab al-Faqih, that he abridged from it his book called Khulasat al-?" . And our master Abd al-Hayy said in Al-Fawa'id that he summarized it from Al-Waqi'at and Al-Khazana, so reflect. And know that he, may Allah have mercy on him, was without peer in his time, unique among the imams of the age, the chief of the Hanafis in Transoxiana. Al-Mawla Ibn Kamal Pasha al-Rumi mentioned him as being from the class of mujtahids in issues who are capable of ijtihad in issues for which there is no narration from the founder of the school, and they are not able to oppose him in furu' and usul. And besides Al-Khulasa, he has acceptable works, including: Khazanat al-Fatawa, and Khazanat al-Waqi'at, and Nisab al-Faqih. And the author of Al-Kashf recorded his death when mentioning those works as the year 542 AH.
Source pages p. 276

Commentary
This passage is a biographical note on the author of Al-Khulasa, a famous Hanafi jurist from Transoxiana. It begins by describing how in the commentary (sharh) various colors are used to highlight the locations of issues, and indexes are placed at the beginning of each book to assist the mufti. It then notes that Al-Khulasa is originally one volume but was printed in India in four volumes. The author also abridged his own work Nisab al-Faqih into Khulasat al-? . According to Abd al-Hayy, he summarized Al-Khulasa from Al-Waqi'at and Al-Khazana. The author is praised as peerless, the foremost of the imams of his time, and the chief of the Hanafis in Transoxiana. Ibn Kamal Pasha al-Rumi classified him as a mujtahid in issues (mujtahid fi al-masa'il) who can perform ijtihad on matters not explicitly narrated from the school's founder, but cannot contradict the founder in furu' and usul. Besides Al-Khulasa, he authored Khazanat al-Fatawa, Khazanat al-Waqi'at, and Nisab al-Faqih. The author of Al-Kashf records his death year as 542 AH.

Key Terms
الخلاصة (Al-Khulasa): A well-known Hanafi fiqh compendium, originally in one volume, abridged from Al-Waqi'at and Al-Khazana.
نصاب الفقيه (Nisab al-Faqih): Another work by the same author, later abridged into Khulasat al-?.
مجتهد في المسائل (mujtahid fi al-masa'il): A jurist capable of ijtihad on new issues not explicitly covered by the school's founder, but bound by the school's principles.

Key Terms from Source Passage

Checkpoint
According to the passage, in what year did the author of Al-Khulasa die?
A) 542 AH
B) 888 AH
C) 1088 AH
D) 885 AH

Key Takeaway
The author of Al-Khulasa was a mujtahid fi al-masa'il from Transoxiana, whose works like Al-Khulasa remain standard Hanafi references, and he died in 542 AH.
